<script>
    window.ramblerToplineParams = { projectName: 'mail', showUser: auth, showLogo: auth, fullWidth: true };


	function setCookie(name, value, options) {
	  options = options || {};

	  var expires = options.expires;

	  if (typeof expires == "number" &amp;&amp; expires) {
	    var d = new Date();
	    d.setTime(d.getTime() + expires * 1000);
	    expires = options.expires = d;
	  }
	  if (expires &amp;&amp; expires.toUTCString) {
	    options.expires = expires.toUTCString();
	  }

	  value = encodeURIComponent(value);

	  var updatedCookie = name + "=" + value;

	  for (var propName in options) {
	    updatedCookie += "; " + propName;
	    var propValue = options[propName];
	    if (propValue !== true) {
	      updatedCookie += "=" + propValue;
	    }
	  }

	  document.cookie = updatedCookie;
	}

	function deleteCookie(name) {
	  setCookie(name, "", {
	    expires: -1
	  })
	}




  </script>

	function setToplineParams(show, goMain) {
		window.ramblerToplineParams.showUser = show;
		window.ramblerToplineParams.showLogo = show;
		if (!goMain) {
			window.location.reload();
		} else {
			localStorage.setItem('out', true);
			window.location.replace('http://www.rambler.ru/?utm_content=head&amp;utm_medium=logo&amp;utm_source=mail&amp;utm_term=redirect');
		}
	}

	if (auth) {
		 document.onreadystatechange = function() {
			if (this.readyState === 'complete' || (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("MSIE 10") !== -1 &amp;&amp; this.readyState === 'loading')) {
				var links = document.getElementsByClassName('rambler-topline-user-dropdown__logout');
				if (links.length &gt; 0) {
					links[0].removeAttribute('href');
				}

				window.ramblerIdHelper.registerOnPossibleLoginCallback(function() {
				       setToplineParams(true, false);
				});
				window.ramblerIdHelper.registerOnPossibleLogoutCallback(function(e, e1) {
					setToplineParams(false, true);
					return false;
				});
			}
		}
	}
</script>
